LU-14980 osd: check for locks in osd_trans_start()

since LU-10048 we shouldn't be starting a transaction with
object (osd) locks held.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2021-09-03 06:16:52.000000000) ---
Patch Set 7:

I guess the question is whether a guaranteed LASSERT() tripping during production is better than a small chance of a lock inversion, but a customer system that keeps running?  I think printing a CERROR() in this case (of maybe CDEBUG(D_ERROR) so it isn't rate limited) referencing LU-14980 would be enough, and if the thread actually hangs then we get a bug report, but otherwise the cluster keeps running...

Optionally, these LASSERTs could be enabled during testing (e.g. if track_declares_assert=1 is set), but not during production?

--- Message (Alex Zhuravlev, 2021-09-03 06:28:51.000000000) ---

well, this patch is rather to catch potential issue. I don't really plan to run it in production.
but I think it's very useful to info the developers about broken rules right away.
we could wrap with with some #if which checks patch level so that released versions have it disabled?
